\newcommand{\WORLD}[1][]{

\begin{document}

\begin{tikzpicture}
\tikzset{set state val/.style args={#1/#2}{#1={fill=brown!#2}}}
\tikzset{set state val/.list={Colombia/100,Canada/50,Russia/20}}
\WORLD[every state={draw=white, thick, fill=black!20}]
